The room facilities are relatively new. The opening is not very large but sufficient. There is a slightly smaller courtyard. There is a capsule coffee machine, ordinary tea bags and coffee bags, Bluetooth speakers, very fast room service, and the robot delivery speed is also very good.
Hygiene: also very good

Let's talk about the shortcomings: catering! I don't know if the entire industry has not paid enough attention to this after the epidemic. Although it can be seen that there are managers patrolling the venue and the service staff are also quite fast in collecting dishes, the buffet of 328 is basically cold and has few choices if it is not the first wave of eating. There is no big difference between breakfast in the morning and in the evening. If it is just a little sashimi, steak and lamb chops, it is really a bit expensive. It can be seen that the Western restaurant still has some pursuit in baking afternoon tea. The desserts are decent and the bread is also made at a certain level, but the Chinese food is really a bit lame. If you have high requirements for eating, you should consider going out to eat, because there is basically no takeaway.
The Chinese restaurant has not yet resumed midnight. I will go there again when I have the chance. Thanks to the service staff for their efforts! Great job!

The horizontal volume of the hotel is very large, the only minor inconvenience is that it is a bit far from the lake view room area to the elevator hall. Other software and hardware belong to the domestic "ceiling" level! I hope that Wanglan can maintain high-quality maintenance for a long time.
